[2025-12-14T23:22:40Z] Kumar Varun: So , Bihar to a large extent ( and a few other eastern Indian states to a lesser extent) use the word Muffasil in police stations unusually more than any other part of the country . ↵ Every town in Bihar will invariably have a Mofussil thana that deals with rural areas attached to the district HQ , as opposed  to Town thana or Sadar etc ↵ Main reason behind it is Bihar’s police structure has changed the slowest since independence and hence retains most of colonial terminology .
